{\footnotesize\ttfamily static void write\+Multi\+Line\+Code\+Link (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2code_8l_a9484188abbc459dafcbd4c96425fa70b}{yyscan\+\_\+t}}}]{yyscanner,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_code_output_interface}{Code\+Output\+Interface}} \&}]{ol,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_definition}{Definition}} $\ast$}]{d,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{text }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

writes a link to a fragment {\itshape text} that may span multiple lines, inserting line numbers for each line. If {\itshape text} contains newlines, the link will be split into multiple links with the same destination, one for each line.
